    FROM [Users] AS [u]
    WHERE [u].[Email] = @__dto_Email_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [RefreshToken] AS [r] ON [t].[Id] = [r].[UserId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id]

            WHERE [p].[value] IS NOT NULL AND (CHARINDEX([p].[value], [c].[TargetProducts]) > 0 OR [p].[value] LIKE N''))) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END
